## This Week in Security: Your News Briefing

Welcome to your weekly security roundup. We've tracked down the **10 most important stories** this
week‚Äîthe ones everyone's talking about, from critical threats to emerging trends that could shape
your security posture. Leading the news this week is **Appsec Roundup - June 2024**, which has
sparked conversation across 9 sources. Meanwhile, the industry is closely tracking **CVE-2025-62673
| TP-Link Archer AX53 v1.0 up to 1.3.1 tdpserver...** with 9 mentions, along with emerging details
on **CVE-2025-58348 | Samsung Mobile Processor/Wearable Processor...**, **Secure by Design roundup -
April 2024**, and **CVE-2025-14321**. Here's the full breakdown of what you need to know.

### üö® Critical Threats This Week

First, the stories that demand your immediate attention:

**1. Appsec Roundup - June 2024**
   Mentioned across 9 industry sources this week. The most important stories around threat modeling, appsec and secure by design for June, 2024.
   [Get the details ‚Üí](https://shostack.org/blog/appsec-roundup-june-2024/)

**2. CVE-2025-62673 | TP-Link Archer AX53 v1.0 up to 1.3.1 tdpserver heap-based overflow**
   Mentioned across 9 industry sources this week. A vulnerability labeled as critical has been found in TP-Link Archer AX53 v1.
   [Get the details ‚Üí](https://nvd.nist.gov/vuln/detail/CVE-2025-62673)

**3. CVE-2025-58348 | Samsung Mobile Processor/Wearable Processor Exynos up to 2200 Wi-Fi Driver confg_tspec memory allocation**
   Mentioned across 9 industry sources this week. A vulnerability identified as problematic has been detected in Samsung Mobile Processor and Wearable Processor Exynos up.
   [Get the details ‚Üí](https://nvd.nist.gov/vuln/detail/CVE-2025-58348)

### üõ†Ô∏è Tools, Updates & Releases

New capabilities and releases worth knowing about:

**1. Secure by Design roundup - April 2024**
   A less busy month in appsec, AI, and regulation, but still interesting stories. Referenced in 6 stories this week.
   [Explore ‚Üí](https://shostack.org/blog/appsec-roundup-april-2024/)

**2. Meeting Third-Party Risk Requirements of DORA in 2026 | UpGuard**
   Learn how to achieve compliance with the third-party risk management standards of the Digital Operat. Referenced in 3 stories this week.
   [Explore ‚Üí](https://upguard-staging.webflow.io/blog/meeting-third-party-risk-requirements-of-dora)

### What You Should Do Next

**Monitor these** in your environment next week:
- Any new CVE announcements related to systems you operate
- Emerging attack techniques being discussed in the community
- Updates and patches for tools your team uses

**Have a look at** the full deep-dives in the trending stories below. Each one provides context that could inform your security decisions this week.
